   <h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en">List of Wimbledon mixed doubles champions</h1> 
   <div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content"> 
    <div id="siteSub" class="noprint">
     From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia
    </div> 
    <div id="contentSub"></div> 
    <div id="jump-to-nav"></div> 
    <a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">Jump to navigation</a> 
    <a class="mw-jump-link" href="#p-search">Jump to search</a> 
    <div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr">
     <div class="mw-parser-output">
      <p>This is a list of the champions and runners-up of the <a href="/wiki/The_Championships,_Wimbledon" title="The Championships, Wimbledon">Wimbledon Championships</a> Mixed Doubles tournament, first introduced to the championship in <a href="/wiki/1913_Wimbledon_Championships" title="1913 Wimbledon Championships">1913</a>. From 1915 to 1918, and from 1940 to 1945, no competition was held due to the two World Wars. </p>
      <p>From 1888, the "All England" mixed doubles championship was held during the <i>Northern Association Tournament</i> (at <a href="/wiki/Manchester" title="Manchester">Manchester</a> or <a href="/wiki/Liverpool" title="Liverpool">Liverpool</a>).<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup> </p> 
      <div id="toc" class="toc">
       <input type="checkbox" role="button" id="toctogglecheckbox" class="toctogglecheckbox" style="display:none">
       <div class="toctitle" lang="en" dir="ltr">
        <h2>Contents</h2>
        <span class="toctogglespan"><label class="toctogglelabel" for="toctogglecheckbox"></label></span>
       </div>

       </ul> 
      </div>

      <div class="thumb tright">
